## Canvas MindMap(æ€ç»´å¯¼å›¾)

### Usage

1. Install the plugin
2. Create a new canvas
3. Create a node in the empty canvas
4. Select the node and the pressÂ `Tab`Â to create a child node (You need to exit edit mode first by pressingÂ `Escape`)
5. Select the child node and pressÂ `Enter`Â to create a brother node
6. Done, you get a mindmap.

### Features

- Auto layout for specific direction
- Select node's tree
- Change color for node's edges

#### Hotkeys

- PressÂ `Enter`Â to create brother card; (You can change this hotkey in setting)
- PressÂ `Tab`Â to create child card;
- PressÂ `Alt`Â +Â `â†/â†’/â†“/â†‘`Â to navigate between nodes;
- PressÂ `Cmd / Ctrl`Â +Â `â†/â†’/â†“/â†‘`Â to create floating nodes;
- PressÂ `Cmd / Ctrl`Â +Â `Shift`Â +Â `â†/â†’/â†“/â†‘`Â to create child nodes;

#### Commands

- Create child node
- Create sibling node
- Create floating node
- Open changelog
- Enter/exit edit mode

#### Showcase

![showcase](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Quorafind/obsidian-canvas-mindmap/master/showcase.gif)

### How to Install

- Obsidian:Â [Available on Obsidian Plugin Market](https://obsidian.md/plugins?id=canvas-mindmap)
- BRAT: AddÂ `quorafind/canvas-mindmap`Â to BRAT.
- Manual: Download the latest release. Extract and put the three files (main.js, manifest.json, styles.css) toÂ `{{obsidian_vault}}/.obsidian/plugins/obsidian-canvas-mindmap`.

## Media Extended(è§†éŸ³é¢‘æ”¯æŒ)

### åŠŸèƒ½ä»‹ç»

![Media Extended plugin with player and media note](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/aidenlx/media-extended/HEAD/first-note.jpg)


Media Extendedæ˜¯ä¸€æ¬¾ä¸“é—¨ä¸ºObsidianè®¾è®¡çš„è§†é¢‘ç¬”è®°æ’ä»¶ï¼Œå®ƒæ”¯æŒç”¨æˆ·åœ¨ç¬”è®°ä¸­æ’å…¥å¹¶æ’­æ”¾è§†é¢‘ï¼ŒåŒæ—¶è¿˜å¯ä»¥è°ƒæ•´è§†é¢‘æ’­æ”¾é€Ÿåº¦ã€æ·»åŠ æ—¶é—´æˆ³ç­‰åŠŸèƒ½ã€‚é€šè¿‡Media Extendedï¼Œç”¨æˆ·å¯ä»¥æ–¹ä¾¿åœ°åœ¨è§‚çœ‹è§†é¢‘çš„è¿‡ç¨‹ä¸­è¿›è¡Œç¬”è®°çš„è®°å½•ä¸æ•´ç†ã€‚

- **Seamless Integration with Obsidian**Â ğŸ¤: Works perfectly with Obsidian's live preview and multi-window support, ensuring a smooth workflow.
- **Embed Multimedia Files**Â ğŸ“: Easily embed both local or hosted video and audio files directly into your notes, bringing your content to life.
- **Playback Control**Â â¯ï¸: Utilize commands and keyboard shortcuts for efficient playback control, including play, pause, skip, and timestamping for quick references.
- **Support for Multiple Video Platforms**Â ğŸŒ: Enjoy support for popular platforms like YouTube, Vimeo, Coursera, Bilibili, and more. If it can be played in a web browser, it can be embedded in your notes.
- **Local Subtitle Support**Â ğŸ“‘: Enhance your media with local subtitle files in SRT, VTT, and ASS formats, making it easier to follow along or understand content in another language.
- **Media Fragments**Â ğŸï¸: Create media fragments that play only within a specified range, perfect for focusing on specific parts of a lecture or presentation.
- **Playlist Support**Â ğŸ“‹: Organize your media files into playlists for continuous playback.

## External PDF(å¤–é“¾PDF)

>ä½¿ç”¨ BRAT æ’ä»¶æ·»åŠ  Git ä»“åº“é“¾æ¥å®‰è£…æ’ä»¶

https://github.com/tenebrisnox/external-PDF-plugin.git
[![external-pdf-logo](https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/89422923/457938116-6ad69920-dc8e-45cb-b6c8-5b0f03e2d2fb.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3NTIzMzM1MTQsIm5iZiI6MTc1MjMzMzIxNCwicGF0aCI6Ii84OTQyMjkyMy80NTc5MzgxMTYtNmFkNjk5MjAtZGM4ZS00NWNiLWI2YzgtNWIwZjAzZTJkMmZiLnBuZz9YLUFtei1BbGdvcml0aG09QVdTNC1ITUFDLVNIQTI1NiZYLUFtei1DcmVkZW50aWFsPUFLSUFWQ09EWUxTQTUzUFFLNFpBJTJGMjAyNTA3MTIlMkZ1cy1lYXN0LTElMkZzMyUyRmF3czRfcmVxdWVzdCZYLUFtei1EYXRlPTIwMjUwNzEyVDE1MTMzNFomWC1BbXotRXhwaXJlcz0zMDAmWC1BbXotU2lnbmF0dXJlPTYyZjljZTBiMmUyNDk2NjI3NjIwMjc3ZWQyZjgyYmE0MDQ2ZWM5MWVkNDA2MDk4ODc0OTc4ZmIxNWFmNmQ3YmMmWC1BbXotU2lnbmVkSGVhZGVycz1ob3N0In0.FWA2Rvcv_Kl6B5QmLNfGUUdEr2-sC-jaVQbcWLeJW0Y)](https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/89422923/457938116-6ad69920-dc8e-45cb-b6c8-5b0f03e2d2fb.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3NTIzMzM1MTQsIm5iZiI6MTc1MjMzMzIxNCwicGF0aCI6Ii84OTQyMjkyMy80NTc5MzgxMTYtNmFkNjk5MjAtZGM4ZS00NWNiLWI2YzgtNWIwZjAzZTJkMmZiLnBuZz9YLUFtei1BbGdvcml0aG09QVdTNC1ITUFDLVNIQTI1NiZYLUFtei1DcmVkZW50aWFsPUFLSUFWQ09EWUxTQTUzUFFLNFpBJTJGMjAyNTA3MTIlMkZ1cy1lYXN0LTElMkZzMyUyRmF3czRfcmVxdWVzdCZYLUFtei1EYXRlPTIwMjUwNzEyVDE1MTMzNFomWC1BbXotRXhwaXJlcz0zMDAmWC1BbXotU2lnbmF0dXJlPTYyZjljZTBiMmUyNDk2NjI3NjIwMjc3ZWQyZjgyYmE0MDQ2ZWM5MWVkNDA2MDk4ODc0OTc4ZmIxNWFmNmQ3YmMmWC1BbXotU2lnbmVkSGVhZGVycz1ob3N0In0.FWA2Rvcv_Kl6B5QmLNfGUUdEr2-sC-jaVQbcWLeJW0Y)

**Embed external PDFs directly into your notes with full viewer controls.**

This plugin lets you embed PDF files hosted online in your Obsidian notes without storing them in your vault. It also allows embedding from local files: either relative to the Obsidian vault or by absolute path (desktop only). It works on mobile devices, too.

[![external-pdf-splash |300](https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/89422923/457968620-16a41a89-adc3-4470-8b61-f21d84998a15.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3NTIzMzM1MTQsIm5iZiI6MTc1MjMzMzIxNCwicGF0aCI6Ii84OTQyMjkyMy80NTc5Njg2MjAtMTZhNDFhODktYWRjMy00NDcwLThiNjEtZjIxZDg0OTk4YTE1LnBuZz9YLUFtei1BbGdvcml0aG09QVdTNC1ITUFDLVNIQTI1NiZYLUFtei1DcmVkZW50aWFsPUFLSUFWQ09EWUxTQTUzUFFLNFpBJTJGMjAyNTA3MTIlMkZ1cy1lYXN0LTElMkZzMyUyRmF3czRfcmVxdWVzdCZYLUFtei1EYXRlPTIwMjUwNzEyVDE1MTMzNFomWC1BbXotRXhwaXJlcz0zMDAmWC1BbXotU2lnbmF0dXJlPTBjNzA0NmM1M2E4NjQ4NmY5MDUxZjMzMTFjOWY5MDMxYjZkNDNkNWYzYzg0MmUwYzkxZTQ5MjM5YWVlZTgyODEmWC1BbXotU2lnbmVkSGVhZGVycz1ob3N0In0.qz0kGThMTvz3vI3usbhejJwckc_o5m2-S_KlQnzP8kg)](https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/89422923/457968620-16a41a89-adc3-4470-8b61-f21d84998a15.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3NTIzMzM1MTQsIm5iZiI6MTc1MjMzMzIxNCwicGF0aCI6Ii84OTQyMjkyMy80NTc5Njg2MjAtMTZhNDFhODktYWRjMy00NDcwLThiNjEtZjIxZDg0OTk4YTE1LnBuZz9YLUFtei1BbGdvcml0aG09QVdTNC1ITUFDLVNIQTI1NiZYLUFtei1DcmVkZW50aWFsPUFLSUFWQ09EWUxTQTUzUFFLNFpBJTJGMjAyNTA3MTIlMkZ1cy1lYXN0LTElMkZzMyUyRmF3czRfcmVxdWVzdCZYLUFtei1EYXRlPTIwMjUwNzEyVDE1MTMzNFomWC1BbXotRXhwaXJlcz0zMDAmWC1BbXotU2lnbmF0dXJlPTBjNzA0NmM1M2E4NjQ4NmY5MDUxZjMzMTFjOWY5MDMxYjZkNDNkNWYzYzg0MmUwYzkxZTQ5MjM5YWVlZTgyODEmWC1BbXotU2lnbmVkSGVhZGVycz1ob3N0In0.qz0kGThMTvz3vI3usbhejJwckc_o5m2-S_KlQnzP8kg)

### How To Use

[](https://github.com/tenebrisnox/external-PDF-plugin?utm_source=chatgpt.com#how-to-use)

### For External PDFs (HTTPS URLs):

[](https://github.com/tenebrisnox/external-PDF-plugin?utm_source=chatgpt.com#for-external-pdfs-https-urls)

````
```external-pdf
https://example.com/document.pdf
title: My Online PDF Document
heght: 500px
```
````

### For Local PDFs in Your Vault (relative path from vault root)

[](https://github.com/tenebrisnox/external-PDF-plugin?utm_source=chatgpt.com#for-local-pdfs-in-your-vault-relative-path-from-vault-root)

````
```external-pdf
Attachements/MyLocalDocument.pdf
title: My Vault PDF Document
heght: 400px
```
````

### For Local PDFs via Absolute Path (desktop only & requires enabling in settings)

[](https://github.com/tenebrisnox/external-PDF-plugin?utm_source=chatgpt.com#for-local-pdfs-via-absolute-path-desktop-only--requires-enabling-in-settings)

````
```external-pdf
/Users/YourName/Documents/AbsolutePathDocument.pdf
title: Absolute Path PDF
heght: 900px
```
````

### Supported Options

[](https://github.com/tenebrisnox/external-PDF-plugin?utm_source=chatgpt.com#supported-options)

- **title:**Â display name for the PDF
- **height:**Â viewer height (eg. 600px, 80vh, 400, 20%)

### Supported Sources

[](https://github.com/tenebrisnox/external-PDF-plugin?utm_source=chatgpt.com#supported-sources)

- local PDF files relative to your Obsidian vault
- local PDF files via absolute path (eg.Â _/mnt/data/report.pdf_) -Â **this is only possible on desktop and requires enabling in settings**.
- Google Drive (sharing links)
- Dropbox (sharing links)
- OneDrive (sharing links)
- GitHub (raw PDF files)
- any direct Https PDF url (for example, one shared by Paperless-NGX)

## Features

[](https://github.com/tenebrisnox/external-PDF-plugin?utm_source=chatgpt.com#features)

- Mobile-optimised with touch gestures (for URLs and vault files).
- Keyboard navigation (arrows, space, +/-, zoom).
- Page comtrols and zoom optons.
- Fit-to-width mode.
- Pinch-to-Zoom on moble.
- Swipe gestures for page navigation.
- Security: the ability to restrict domains (for external URLs)

### Settings

[](https://github.com/tenebrisnox/external-PDF-plugin?utm_source=chatgpt.com#settings)

## Templater

![templater_logo](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SilentVoid13/Templater/HEAD/imgs/templater_logo.svg)

[Templater](https://github.com/SilentVoid13/Templater)Â is a template plugin forÂ [Obsidian.md](https://obsidian.md/). It defines a templating language that lets you insert variables and functions results into your notes. It will also let you execute JavaScript code manipulating those variables and functions.

### Documentation

Check out the completeÂ [documentation](https://silentvoid13.github.io/Templater/)Â to start usingÂ [Templater](https://github.com/SilentVoid13/Templater).

### Warning

[Templater](https://github.com/SilentVoid13/Templater)Â allows you to execute arbitrary JavaScript code and system commands.

It can be dangerous to execute arbitrary JavaScript code or system commands from untrusted sources. Only run code / commands that you understand, from trusted sources.

### Template Showcase / Questions / Ideas / Help

Go to theÂ [discussion](https://github.com/SilentVoid13/Templater/discussions)Â tab to ask and find this kind of things.

Don't be shy and share your templates created usingÂ [Templater](https://github.com/SilentVoid13/Templater)Â in theÂ [Template Showcase](https://github.com/SilentVoid13/Templater/discussions/categories/templates-showcase)Â category. UseÂ [gists](https://gist.github.com/)Â to share the template file.

## Calibre(Calibre è”åŠ¨)

This is a calibre Content server plugin forÂ [Obsidian](https://obsidian.md/). Allow you to access your calibre libraries and read books directly in Obsidian. Rearrange a comfortable layout of the workspace, you can take notes while reading, and read more books at the same time by opening more panes.

- [Obsidian Calibre Plugin](app://obsidian.md/index.html#obsidian-calibre-plugin)
    - [How it Works](app://obsidian.md/index.html#how-it-works)
    - [How to use](app://obsidian.md/index.html#how-to-use)
        - [Start quickly](app://obsidian.md/index.html#start-quickly)
            - [STEP 1: Start Content Server](app://obsidian.md/index.html#step-1-start-content-server)
            - [STEP 2: Install Calibre Plugin](app://obsidian.md/index.html#step-2-install-calibre-plugin)
            - [STEP 3: Open Calibre Container](app://obsidian.md/index.html#step-3-open-calibre-container)
        - [How to Change Content Server Port](app://obsidian.md/index.html#how-to-change-content-server-port)
            - [Change in Calibre Application](app://obsidian.md/index.html#change-in-calibre-application)
            - [Change in Calibre Plugin](app://obsidian.md/index.html#change-in-calibre-plugin)
    - [Manually installing the plugin](app://obsidian.md/index.html#manually-installing-the-plugin)
    - [The calibre Content server](app://obsidian.md/index.html#the-calibre-content-server)

### How it Works

Calibre plugin will open a Obsidian view in your workspace when you click Calibre ribbon icon. The view contains an iframe to connect to the content server. You can change the server address in plugin settings.

### How to use

#### Start quickly

##### STEP 1: Start Content Server

To start the server, click the Connect/share button and choose Start Content server.

![image](https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/150803/143490663-afc3b418-a36e-422a-bab7-97b09237b507.png)

##### STEP 2: Install Calibre Plugin

Just do it.

##### STEP 3: Open Calibre Container

Click the ribbon icon to open Calibre Container.

![image](https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/150803/143490701-b7eedf79-b555-49e7-ad67-1a55da714c46.png)

![image](https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/150803/143516737-05d428df-88fc-40a9-a26b-cd163683d607.png)

#### How to Change Content Server Port

##### Change in Calibre Application

![image](https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/150803/143490820-094fd57d-8150-4b82-a678-a81e3f15614e.png)

![image](https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/150803/143490891-58dcb930-c0c6-40ee-9256-ab25164a77ec.png)

##### Change in Calibre Plugin

![image](https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/150803/143490977-89e98839-0861-44c5-a002-b855a26f00ae.png)

### Manually installing the plugin

- Copy overÂ `main.js`,Â `styles.css`,Â `manifest.json`Â fromÂ [Releases](https://github.com/caronchen/obsidian-calibre-plugin/releases)Â to your vaultÂ `VaultFolder/.obsidian/plugins/obsidian-calibre-plugin/`.

### The calibre Content server

SeeÂ [https://manual.calibre-ebook.com/server.html](https://manual.calibre-ebook.com/server.html)

## Iconize(æ–‡ä»¶å›¾æ ‡)

![Preview Image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/FlorianWoelki/obsidian-iconize/HEAD/docs/preview-image.png)

Project Deprecation and End of Maintenance:Â [read more](https://github.com/FlorianWoelki/obsidian-iconize/discussions/646)

## What is it?

This obsidian plugin allows you to addÂ **any**Â custom icon (of typeÂ `.svg`) or from an icon pack to anything you want.

Refer to the official documentation for more information:  
[https://florianwoelki.github.io/obsidian-iconize/](https://florianwoelki.github.io/obsidian-iconize/)Â about the plugin and its functionalities.

If you like this plugin, feel free to support the development by buying a coffee:

[![Buy Me A Coffee](https://cdn.buymeacoffee.com/buttons/v2/default-yellow.png)](https://www.buymeacoffee.com/florianwoelki)

## Key Highlights

[Icons before file/folder name](https://florianwoelki.github.io/obsidian-iconize/files-and-folders/icon-before-file-or-folder.html),  
[Icons in notes](https://florianwoelki.github.io/obsidian-iconize/notes/icons-in-notes.html),  
[Icon above title](https://florianwoelki.github.io/obsidian-iconize/notes/title-icon.html),  
[Predefined icon packs](https://florianwoelki.github.io/obsidian-iconize/guide/icon-packs.html),  
[Icons in tabs](https://florianwoelki.github.io/obsidian-iconize/files-and-folders/icon-tabs.html),  
[Customizable settings](https://florianwoelki.github.io/obsidian-iconize/guide/settings.html),  
[Custom rules](https://florianwoelki.github.io/obsidian-iconize/files-and-folders/custom-rules.html),  
[Frontmatter integration](https://florianwoelki.github.io/obsidian-iconize/files-and-folders/use-frontmatter.html),  
[Change color of an individual icon](https://florianwoelki.github.io/obsidian-iconize/files-and-folders/individual-icon-color.html),

## Development

To customize this project for your needs, you can clone it and then install all dependencies:

```sh
$ git clone https://github.com/FlorianWoelki/obsidian-iconize
$ cd obsidian-iconize
$ pnpm i
```

After the installation, you need to create aÂ `env.js`Â file in the root directory. Fill the file with the following content:

```js
export const obsidianExportPath =
  '<path-to-obsidian-vault>/.obsidian/plugins/obsidian-iconize/';
```

Make sure you create the directory specified in that variable if it does not exist yet.

Afterwards, you can start the rollup dev server by using:

```sh
$ pnpm dev
```

This command will automatically build the neccesary files for testing and developing on every change. Furthermore, it does copy all the necessary files to the plugin directory you specified.

Finally, you can customize the plugin and add it to your plugins.
